   390             imageUrl={config.watermark.imageUrl}
   391             opacity={config.watermark.opacity}
   392             position={config.watermark.position}
   393             scale={config.watermark.scale}
   394           />
   395         )}
   396       </div>
   397     </div>
   398   );
   399 };
   400 
   401 interface WatermarkLayerProps {
   402   imageUrl: string;
   403   opacity: number;
   404   position: string;
   405   scale: number;
   406 }
   407 
   408 const WatermarkLayer: React.FC<WatermarkLayerProps> = ({ imageUrl, opacity, position, scale }) => {
   409   const positionStyles: Record<string, React.CSSProperties> = {
   410     center: { top: '50%', left: '50%', transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)' },
   411     'bottom-right': { bottom: '20px', right: '20px' },
   412     'bottom-left': { bottom: '20px', left: '20px' },
   413     'top-right': { top: '20px', right: '20px' },
   414     tile: { top: 0, left: 0, width: '100%', height: '100%', backgroundImage: `url(${imageUrl})`, backgroundRepeat: 'repeat', backgroundSize: `${scale * 120}px` },
   415   };
   416 
   417   if (position === 'tile') {
   418     return (
   419       <div
   420         style={{
   421           position: 'absolute',
   422           ...positionStyles.tile,
   423           opacity,
   424           pointerEvents: 'none',
   425           zIndex: 10,
   426         }}
   427       />
   428     );
   429   }
   430 
   431   return (
   432     <img
   433       src={imageUrl}
   434       alt="水印"
   435       style={{
   436         position: 'absolute',
   437         ...positionStyles[position],
   438         opacity,
   439         pointerEvents: 'none',
   440         zIndex: 10,
   441         width: `${scale * 100}%`,
   442         maxWidth: '200px',
   443       }}
   444     />
   445   );
   446 };

   448 export default CardPreview;

     8 import type { ExportFormat, ExportQuality } from '@/types/card';
     9 import { toast } from 'sonner';
    10 
    11 interface ExportDialogProps {
    12   previewRef: React.RefObject<HTMLDivElement | null>;
    13 }
    14 
    15 // 子组件定义在组件外部，避免每次 ExportDialog 渲染产生新类型导致 React 卸载重挂载
    16 const OptionGroup: React.FC<{ label: string; children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ label, children }) => (

    30 const OptionBtn: React.FC<OptionBtnProps> = ({ active, onClick, children, badge }) => (

    45   </button>

    47 
    48 const ExportDialog: React.FC<ExportDialogProps> = ({ previewRef }) => {
    49   const [format, setFormat] = useState<ExportFormat>('png');
    50   const [quality, setQuality] = useState<ExportQuality>('hd');
    51   const [isExporting, setIsExporting] = useState(false);
    52   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
    53 
    54   const qualityOptions: { value: ExportQuality; label: string; scale: number; badge?: string }[] = [
    55     { value: 'hd',      label: '高清',   scale: 3 },
    56     { value: 'ultra',   label: '超清',   scale: 4 },
    57     { value: 'extreme', label: '极致',   scale: 5, badge: 'HOT' },
    58     { value: 'pro',     label: '专业',   scale: 6, badge: 'PRO' },
    59   ];
    60 
    61   const handleExport = async () => {
    62     const el = previewRef.current;
    63     if (!el) {
    64       toast.error('找不到预览区域');
    65       return;
    66     }
    67 
    68     const scale = qualityOptions.find(q => q.value === quality)?.scale ?? 3;
    69 
    70     // 导出前估算内存占用：pixelRatio^2 × DOM 面积 × 4 字节/像素
    71     const estimatedW = (el.offsetWidth || 440) * scale;
    72     const estimatedH = (el.offsetHeight || 600) * scale;
    73     const estimatedMB = (estimatedW * estimatedH * 4) / (1024 * 1024);
    74     if (estimatedMB > 25) {
    75       toast.warning(
    76         `当前清晰度（×${scale}）预计生成 ${Math.round(estimatedMB)} MB 图片，低配设备可能较慢`,
    77         { duration: 4000 }
    78       );
    79     }
    80 
    81     setIsExporting(true);
    82     try {
    83       const opts = {
    84         pixelRatio: scale,
    85         cacheBust: true,
    86         skipAutoScale: false,
    87         backgroundColor: format === 'jpg' ? '#FFFFFF' : undefined,
    88       };
    89 
    90       // 15 秒超时保护：html-to-image 在跨域资源/字体未就绪/CSS filter 时会无限挂起
    91       const TIMEOUT_MS = 15_000;
    92       let timeoutId: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>;
    93       const timeout = new Promise<never>((_, reject) => {
    94         timeoutId = setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('导出超时')), TIMEOUT_MS);
    95       });
    96 
    97       let dataUrl: string;
    98       try {
    99         if (format === 'png') {
   100           dataUrl = await Promise.race([toPng(el, opts), timeout]);
   101         } else {
   102           dataUrl = await Promise.race([toJpeg(el, { ...opts, quality: 0.92 }), timeout]);
   103         }
   104       } finally {
   105         // 无论成功/失败，立即清理悬挂的超时定时器，避免 15s 后的无效 reject
   106         clearTimeout(timeoutId!);
   107       }
   108 
   109       const link = document.createElement('a');
   110       link.download = `墨迹文卡_${Date.now()}.${format}`;
   111       link.href = dataUrl;
   112       link.click();
   113 
   114       toast.success(`导出成功！格式：${format.toUpperCase()}，清晰度：${qualityOptions.find(q => q.value === quality)?.label ?? quality}`);
   115       setOpen(false);
   116     } catch (err) {
   117       console.error('导出失败', err);
   118       const isTimeout = err instanceof Error && err.message === '导出超时';
   119       toast.error(
   120         isTimeout
   121           ? '导出超时（15s），请尝试降低清晰度或减少图片数量'
   122           : '导出失败，请重试'
   123       );
   124     } finally {
   125       setIsExporting(false);
   126     }
   127   };
   128 
   129   return (
   130     <Popover open={open} onOpenChange={setOpen}>
   131       <div className="flex items-stretch">
   132         <Button
   133           onClick={() => setOpen(true)}
   134           className="rounded-r-none pr-3 gap-1.5 font-medium"
   135           disabled={isExporting}
   136         >
   137           {isExporting ? <Loader2 size={14} className="animate-spin" /> : <Download size={14} />}
   138           导出
   139         </Button>
   140         <PopoverTrigger asChild>
   141           <Button
   142             className="rounded-l-none pl-2 pr-2.5 border-l border-primary-foreground/30"
   143             disabled={isExporting}
   144           >
   145             <ChevronDown size={14} />
   146           </Button>
   147         </PopoverTrigger>
   148       </div>
   149 
   150       <PopoverContent align="end" className="w-72 p-4">
   151         <div className="mb-3">
   152           <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-foreground">导出设置</h3>
   153         </div>
   154 
   155         <OptionGroup label="导出格式">
   156           <OptionBtn active={format === 'png'} onClick={() => setFormat('png')}>PNG</OptionBtn>
   157           <OptionBtn active={format === 'jpg'} onClick={() => setFormat('jpg')}>JPG</OptionBtn>
   158         </OptionGroup>
   159 
   160         <OptionGroup label="清晰度">
   161           {qualityOptions.map(opt => (
   162             <OptionBtn
   163               key={opt.value}
   164               active={quality === opt.value}
   165               onClick={() => setQuality(opt.value)}
   166               badge={opt.badge}
   167             >
   168               {opt.label}
   169             </OptionBtn>
   170           ))}
   171         </OptionGroup>
   172 
   173         <Button
   174           className="w-full mt-1 gap-2"
   175           onClick={handleExport}
   176           disabled={isExporting}
   177         >
   178           {isExporting ? (
   179             <><Loader2 size={14} className="animate-spin" />导出中...</>
   180           ) : (
   181             <><Download size={14} />开始导出</>
   182           )}
   183         </Button>
   184       </PopoverContent>
   185     </Popover>
   186   );
   187 };

     2 // - 有选中文字：对选区应用 setFontFamily（局部字体）

     6 import { Type, Upload, X, Check, ChevronDown } from 'lucide-react';
     7 import { useFontManager, type FontItem } from '@/hooks/useFontManager';

    16 
    17 interface FontPickerProps {
    18   // 当前全局字体 family
    19   globalFont: string;
    20   onGlobalFontChange: (family: string) => void;
    21   // TipTap editor 实例，用于判断是否有选区

    24 
    25 const FontPicker: React.FC<FontPickerProps> = ({
    26   globalFont,
    27   onGlobalFontChange,
    28   editor,
    29 }) => {
    30   const { allFonts, uploadFont, deleteFont } = useFontManager();
    31   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
    32   const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);
    33   const [hoveredId, setHoveredId] = useState<string | null>(null);
    34 
    35   // 当前激活字体名称（用于按钮显示）
    36   const activeFont = allFonts.find(f => f.family === globalFont);
    37 
    38   const handleSelect = (font: FontItem) => {
    39     // 判断编辑器是否有文字选区
    40     const hasSelection =
    41       editor &&
    42       !editor.state.selection.empty;
    43 
    44     if (hasSelection && editor) {
    45       // 局部模式：对选区应用字体
    46       editor.chain().focus().setFontFamily(font.family).run();
    47       toast.success(`已对选中文字应用「${font.name}」`);
    48     } else {
    49       // 全局模式：切换全文字体
    50       onGlobalFontChange(font.family);
    51       toast.success(`全文字体已切换为「${font.name}」`);
    52     }
    53     setOpen(false);
    54   };
    55 
    56   const handleUpload = async () => {
    57     setUploading(true);
    58     try {
    59       const font = await uploadFont();
    60       if (font) {
    61         toast.success(`字体「${font.name}」上传成功`);
    62       }
    63     } finally {
    64       setUploading(false);
    65     }
    66   };
    67 
    68   const handleDelete = (e: React.MouseEvent, id: string, name: string) => {
    69     e.stopPropagation();
    70     deleteFont(id);
    71     toast.success(`已删除字体「${name}」`);
    72   };
    73 
    74   const builtinFonts = allFonts.filter(f => f.isBuiltin);
    75   const customFonts = allFonts.filter(f => !f.isBuiltin);
    76 
    77   return (
    78     <Popover open={open} onOpenChange={setOpen}>
    79       <PopoverTrigger asChild>
    80         <button

    82           title="字体"

    95         {builtinFonts.map(font => (
    96           <FontRow
    97             key={font.id}
    98             font={font}
    99             isActive={globalFont === font.family}
   100             hovered={hoveredId === font.id}
   101             onHover={setHoveredId}
   102             onSelect={handleSelect}
   103             onDelete={handleDelete}

   111             <div className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground px-2 py-1 font-medium">自定义字体</div>
   112             {customFonts.map(font => (

   114                 key={font.id}

   116                 isActive={globalFont === font.family}
   117                 hovered={hoveredId === font.id}
   118                 onHover={setHoveredId}
   119                 onSelect={handleSelect}
   120                 onDelete={handleDelete}
   121                 showDelete

   123             ))}
   124           </>

   126

   129         <button
   130           onClick={handleUpload}
   131           disabled={uploading}
   132           className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1.5 rounded text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-foreground transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
   133         >

   136           <span className="ml-auto text-[10px] opacity-60">ttf/otf/woff</span>

   143 // ────────────────────────────────────────────────

   146 interface FontRowProps {
   147   font: FontItem;
   148   isActive: boolean;
   149   hovered: boolean;
   150   onHover: (id: string | null) => void;
   151   onSelect: (font: FontItem) => void;
   152   onDelete?: (e: React.MouseEvent, id: string, name: string) => void;
   153   showDelete?: boolean;
   154 }
   155 
   156 const FontRow: React.FC<FontRowProps> = ({
   157   font, isActive, hovered, onHover, onSelect, onDelete, showDelete = false,
   158 }) => (
   159   <div
   160     className="relative flex items-center"
   161     onMouseEnter={() => onHover(font.id)}
   162     onMouseLeave={() => onHover(null)}
   163   >
   164     <button
   165       onClick={() => onSelect(font)}
   166       className={`flex-1 flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1.5 rounded text-xs transition-colors text-left ${
   167         isActive
   168           ? 'bg-primary/10 text-foreground'
   169           : 'text-foreground hover:bg-accent'
   170       }`}
   171       style={{ fontFamily: font.family }}

   174       {!isActive && <span className="w-[11px] shrink-0" />}
   175       <span className="truncate">{font.name}</span>
   176     </button>
   177 
   178     {/* 悬浮删除按钮（仅自定义字体） */}
   179     {showDelete && onDelete && hovered && (

     1 // 字体管理 Hook：内置字体 + 自定义上传
     2 // 字体 base64 存储于 IndexedDB（避免 localStorage ~5MB 溢出）
     3 import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
     4 
     5 export interface FontItem {
     6   id: string;
     7   name: string;         // 显示名称
     8   family: string;       // CSS font-family 值
     9   isBuiltin: boolean;   // 是否内置字体
    10   dataUrl?: string;     // 自定义字体的 base64 data URL（仅 IndexedDB 内存储）
    11 }
    12 
    13 // localStorage 中仅保留轻量元数据（无 dataUrl），用于展示字体列表
    14 interface FontMeta {
    15   id: string;
    16   name: string;
    17   family: string;
    18 }
    19 
    20 const DB_NAME = 'mojika_fonts_db';
    21 const DB_VERSION = 1;
    22 const STORE_NAME = 'custom_fonts';
    23 const META_KEY = 'mojika_custom_fonts_meta';   // localStorage key（仅存元数据）
    24 const LEGACY_KEY = 'mojika_custom_fonts';       // 旧版 localStorage key（含 base64）
    25 
    26 // ─── IndexedDB helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    27 
    28 // 模块级连接缓存：所有操作复用同一个 Promise<IDBDatabase>，
    29 // 避免每次 dbGetAll/dbPut/dbDelete 都发起新的 indexedDB.open() 握手，
    30 // 防止移动端并发 open 时触发 "The database connection is closing" 异常。
    31 let dbPromise: Promise<IDBDatabase> | null = null;
    32 
    33 function getDB(): Promise<IDBDatabase> {
    34   if (!dbPromise) {
    35     dbPromise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    36       const req = indexedDB.open(DB_NAME, DB_VERSION);
    37       req.onupgradeneeded = (e) => {
    38         const db = (e.target as IDBOpenDBRequest).result;
    39         if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE_NAME)) {
    40           db.createObjectStore(STORE_NAME, { keyPath: 'id' });
    41         }
    42       };
    43       req.onsuccess = () => resolve(req.result);
    44       req.onerror = () => {
    45         dbPromise = null; // 打开失败时重置，允许下次重试
    46         reject(req.error);
    47       };
    48     });
    49   }
    50   return dbPromise;
    51 }
    52 
    53 /**
    54  * InvalidStateError 自恢复：iOS Safari 在内存压力下会强制关闭 DB 连接。
    55  * 后续事务会抛出 InvalidStateError（"The database connection is closing"）。
    56  * 检测到此错误时重置 dbPromise，使下一次调用重新 open DB。
    57  */
    58 function handleDbError(err: unknown): void {
    59   if (err instanceof DOMException && err.name === 'InvalidStateError') {
    60     dbPromise = null;
    61   }
    62 }
    63 
    64 async function dbGetAll(): Promise<FontItem[]> {
    65   try {
    66     const db = await getDB();
    67     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    68       const tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, 'readonly');
    69       const req = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME).getAll();
    70       req.onsuccess = () => resolve((req.result ?? []) as FontItem[]);
    71       req.onerror = () => { handleDbError(req.error); reject(req.error); };
    72     });
    73   } catch (err) {
    74     handleDbError(err);
    75     return [];
    76   }
    77 }
    78 
    79 async function dbPut(font: FontItem): Promise<void> {
    80   const db = await getDB();
    81   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    82     const tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, 'readwrite');
    83     const req = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME).put(font);
    84     req.onsuccess = () => resolve();
    85     req.onerror = () => { handleDbError(req.error); reject(req.error); };
    86   });
    87 }
    88 
    89 async function dbDelete(id: string): Promise<void> {
    90   const db = await getDB();
    91   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    92     const tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, 'readwrite');
    93     const req = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME).delete(id);
    94     req.onsuccess = () => resolve();
    95     req.onerror = () => { handleDbError(req.error); reject(req.error); };
    96   });
    97 }
    98 
    99 // ─── 元数据 helpers（localStorage，仅存 id/name/family）─────────────────────
   100 
   101 function loadFontMeta(): FontMeta[] {
   102   try {
   103     const raw = localStorage.getItem(META_KEY);
   104     return raw ? (JSON.parse(raw) as FontMeta[]) : [];
   105   } catch {
   106     return [];
   107   }
   108 }
   109 
   110 function saveFontMeta(fonts: FontItem[]): void {
   111   try {
   112     const meta: FontMeta[] = fonts.map(({ id, name, family }) => ({ id, name, family }));
   113     localStorage.setItem(META_KEY, JSON.stringify(meta));
   114   } catch {
   115     console.warn('字体元数据保存失败');
   116   }
   117 }
   118 
   119 // ─── 旧版 localStorage 数据迁移 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   120 
   121 async function migrateLegacyStorage(): Promise<void> {
   122   try {
   123     const raw = localStorage.getItem(LEGACY_KEY);
   124     if (!raw) return;
   125     const fonts = JSON.parse(raw) as FontItem[];
   126     // 保证原子性：全部写入 IndexedDB 成功后才删除旧 localStorage 数据。
   127     // 若 Promise.all 中途失败，localStorage 保留原始数据，下次启动可重试迁移。
   128     await Promise.all(fonts.map(f => dbPut(f)));
   129     saveFontMeta(fonts);
   130     localStorage.removeItem(LEGACY_KEY);
   131   } catch {
   132     // 迁移失败不影响正常使用；旧数据保留，下次启动重试
   133   }
   134 }
   135 
   136 // ─── 内置字体 ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   137 
   138 export const BUILTIN_FONTS: FontItem[] = [
   139   { id: 'source-han-sans', name: '思源黑体', family: '"Source Han Sans CN", "Noto Sans CJK SC", "PingFang SC", "Microsoft YaHei", sans-serif', isBuiltin: true },
   140   { id: 'source-han-serif', name: '思源宋体', family: '"Source Han Serif CN", "Noto Serif CJK SC", "SimSun", serif', isBuiltin: true },
   141   { id: 'kaiti', name: '楷体', family: '"KaiTi", "楷体", "STKaiti", "AR PL UKai CN", serif', isBuiltin: true },
   142   { id: 'simsun', name: '宋体', family: '"SimSun", "宋体", "STSong", serif', isBuiltin: true },
   143   { id: 'microsoft-yahei', name: '微软雅黑', family: '"Microsoft YaHei", "微软雅黑", "PingFang SC", sans-serif', isBuiltin: true },
   144 ];
   145 
   146 // ─── FontFace 注册（带并发去重）───────────────────────────────────────────────
   147 
   148 const registeringFonts = new Map<string, Promise<void>>();
   149 
   150 function registerFontFace(font: FontItem): Promise<void> {
   151   if (!font.dataUrl) return Promise.resolve();
   152   if ([...document.fonts].some(f => f.family === `"${font.family}"`)) return Promise.resolve();
   153 
   154   const inflight = registeringFonts.get(font.family);
   155   if (inflight) return inflight;
   156 
   157   const p = (async () => {
   158     try {
   159       const ff = new FontFace(font.family, `url(${font.dataUrl})`);
   160       await ff.load();
   161       document.fonts.add(ff);
   162     } catch {
   163       console.warn(`字体 ${font.name} 注册失败`);
   164     } finally {
   165       registeringFonts.delete(font.family);
   166     }
   167   })();
   168 
   169   registeringFonts.set(font.family, p);
   170   return p;
   171 }
   172 
   173 // ─── Hook ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   174 
   175 export function useFontManager() {
   176   // 初始值从 localStorage 元数据快速恢复（无 dataUrl），避免首帧闪空
   177   const [customFonts, setCustomFonts] = useState<FontItem[]>(() =>
   178     loadFontMeta().map(m => ({ ...m, isBuiltin: false }))
   179   );
   180 
   181   useEffect(() => {
   182     (async () => {
   183       // 迁移旧版 localStorage base64 数据至 IndexedDB
   184       await migrateLegacyStorage();
   185       // 从 IndexedDB 加载完整数据（含 dataUrl）并注册字体
   186       const fonts = await dbGetAll();
   187       if (fonts.length) {
   188         setCustomFonts(fonts);
   189         fonts.forEach(f => registerFontFace(f));
   190       }
   191     })();
   192   }, []);
   193 
   194   const allFonts: FontItem[] = [...BUILTIN_FONTS, ...customFonts];
   195 
   196   const uploadFont = useCallback((): Promise<FontItem | null> => {
   197     return new Promise((resolve) => {
   198       const input = document.createElement('input');
   199       input.type = 'file';
   200       input.accept = '.ttf,.otf,.woff,.woff2';
   201 
   202       // 用户取消文件选择对话框时 resolve(null)，避免 Promise 永久悬挂
   203       // 'cancel' 事件：Chrome 113+，Safari 16.4+，Firefox 91+（主流版本均已支持）
   204       // window focus 兜底：对话框关闭时 window 重新获得焦点（覆盖更旧的浏览器）
   205       const onCancel = () => { cleanup(); resolve(null); };
   206       const onWindowFocus = () => {
   207         // 延迟 300ms：onchange 可能在 focus 后触发，避免误判为取消
   208         setTimeout(() => {
   209           if (!input.files?.length) { cleanup(); resolve(null); }
   210         }, 300);
   211       };
   212       const cleanup = () => {
   213         input.removeEventListener('cancel', onCancel);
   214         window.removeEventListener('focus', onWindowFocus);
   215       };
   216 
   217       input.addEventListener('cancel', onCancel);
   218       window.addEventListener('focus', onWindowFocus, { once: true });
   219 
   220       input.onchange = async (e) => {
   221         cleanup();
   222         const file = (e.target as HTMLInputElement).files?.[0];
   223         if (!file) { resolve(null); return; }
   224 
   225         const ext = file.name.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase() ?? 'ttf';
   226         const mimeMap: Record<string, string> = {
   227           ttf: 'font/truetype', otf: 'font/otf',
   228           woff: 'font/woff', woff2: 'font/woff2',
   229         };
   230         const mime = mimeMap[ext] ?? 'font/truetype';
   231 
   232         const reader = new FileReader();
   233         reader.onload = async (ev) => {
   234           const dataUrl = (ev.target?.result as string)
   235             .replace(/^data:[^;]+/, `data:${mime}`);
   236           const newFont: FontItem = {
   237             id: `custom_${Date.now()}`,
   238             name: file.name.replace(/\.[^.]+$/, ''),
   239             family: `CustomFont_${Date.now()}`,
   240             isBuiltin: false,
   241             dataUrl,
   242           };
   243 
   244           // 先写 IndexedDB，再注册到浏览器，最后更新 state + 元数据
   245           // 若 dbPut 失败（如 QuotaExceededError），resolve(null) 而非更新 state，
   246           // 避免内存状态与 IndexedDB 不同步（页面刷新后字体消失但列表显示有）
   247           try {
   248             await dbPut(newFont);
   249           } catch (e) {
   250             console.warn('字体写入 IndexedDB 失败，已取消上传:', e);
   251             resolve(null);
   252             return;
   253           }
   254 
   255           await registerFontFace(newFont);
   256 
   257           setCustomFonts(prev => {
   258             const updated = [...prev, newFont];
   259             saveFontMeta(updated);
   260             return updated;
   261           });
   262           resolve(newFont);
   263         };
   264         // 字体文件损坏或读取中断时，resolve(null) 而非永久悬挂
   265         reader.onerror = () => { resolve(null); };
   266         reader.readAsDataURL(file);
   267       };
   268       input.click();
   269     });
   270   }, []);
   271 
   272   const deleteFont = useCallback((id: string) => {
   273     // 乐观更新：先从 state 移除（UI 立即响应），再异步删除 IndexedDB
   274     // 若 DB 删除失败，回滚 state（避免"鬼字体"：state 已删但 DB 仍存，刷新后复活）
   275     setCustomFonts(prev => {
   276       const rollback = prev;
   277       const updated = prev.filter(f => f.id !== id);
   278       saveFontMeta(updated);
   279 
   280       dbDelete(id).catch((e) => {
   281         console.warn('字体删除 IndexedDB 失败，已回滚:', e);
   282         setCustomFonts(rollback);
   283         saveFontMeta(rollback);
   284       });
   285 
   286       return updated;
   287     });
   288   }, []);
   289 
   290   return { allFonts, customFonts, uploadFont, deleteFont };
   291 }

     1 import MarkdownIt from 'markdown-it';
     2 import hljs from 'highlight.js';
     3 import type { TemplateStyles } from '@/types/card';
     4 
     5 const md: MarkdownIt = new MarkdownIt({
     6   html: true,
     7   linkify: true,
     8   typographer: true,
     9   highlight: (str: string, lang: string): string => {
    10     if (lang && hljs.getLanguage(lang)) {
    11       try {
    12         return `<pre class="hljs-pre"><code class="hljs language-${lang}">${hljs.highlight(str, { language: lang, ignoreIllegals: true }).value}</code></pre>`;
    13       } catch {
    14         // fall through
    15       }
    16     }
    17     return `<pre class="hljs-pre"><code class="hljs">${md.utils.escapeHtml(str)}</code></pre>`;
    18   },
    19 });
    20 
    21 /**
    22  * 模块级渲染缓存（LRU-lite）。
    23  *
    24  * 问题背景：
    25  *   md.render() 包含词法分析 + 语法树构建 + HTML 生成 + highlight.js 代码着色，
    26  *   是整个预览流水线中最重的 CPU 操作。每次 React 重渲染（模板切换、字体调整、
    27  *   水印开关等）都会触发一次完整渲染，即使 markdown 内容完全未变。
    28  *
    29  * 方案：Map 固定容量 = 16 条，超出后删除最早插入项（FIFO 近似 LRU）。
    30  *   - 16 条约覆盖单次会话内的全部历史输入，命中率接近 100%。
    31  *   - Map 保存的是纯字符串（key + value），内存上限约 16 × 平均文档大小。
    32  *   - 不使用 WeakMap（key 为 string，非对象）。
    33  */
    34 const RENDER_CACHE_MAX = 16;
    35 const renderCache = new Map<string, string>();
    36 
    37 function cachedRender(text: string): string {
    38   const hit = renderCache.get(text);
    39   if (hit !== undefined) return hit;
    40 
    41   const result = md.render(text);
    42 
    43   if (renderCache.size >= RENDER_CACHE_MAX) {
    44     // 删除最早插入的 key（Map 迭代顺序 = 插入顺序）
    45     renderCache.delete(renderCache.keys().next().value!);
    46   }
    47   renderCache.set(text, result);
    48   return result;
    49 }
    50 
    51 // 自定义渲染器
    52 export function renderMarkdown(text: string): string {
    53   return cachedRender(text);
    54 }
    55 
    56 export function getTemplateContentStyles(styles: TemplateStyles, font: { baseFontSize: number; titleLinked: boolean; titleFontSize: number; tableLinked: boolean; tableFontSize: number }): Record<string, string> {
    57   const titleMultiplier = font.titleLinked ? font.titleFontSize : font.titleFontSize / font.baseFontSize;
    58   const tableMultiplier = font.tableLinked ? font.tableFontSize : font.tableFontSize / font.baseFontSize;
    59 
    60   return {
    61     '--tpl-title': styles.titleColor,
    62     '--tpl-text': styles.textColor,
    63     '--tpl-accent': styles.accentColor,
    64     '--tpl-list-num-bg': styles.listNumberBg,
    65     '--tpl-list-num-color': styles.listNumberColor,
    66     '--tpl-bullet': styles.bulletColor,
    67     '--tpl-quote-border': styles.blockquoteBorder,
    68     '--tpl-quote-text': styles.blockquoteText ?? styles.textColor,
    69     '--tpl-code-bg': styles.codeBg,
    70     '--tpl-code-text': styles.codeText,
    71     '--tpl-divider': styles.dividerColor ?? `${styles.textColor}33`,
    72     '--tpl-title-size': `${titleMultiplier * 1.2}em`,
    73     '--tpl-h2-size': `${titleMultiplier * 1.0}em`,
    74     '--tpl-h3-size': `${titleMultiplier * 0.85}em`,
    75     '--tpl-table-size': `${tableMultiplier}em`,
    76   };
    77 }

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-byyhgn8k5lhd/src/components/common/ErrorBoundary.tsx:
     1 import React from 'react';
     2 import { AlertTriangle, RotateCcw } from 'lucide-react';
     3 import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
     4 
     5 interface ErrorBoundaryProps {
     6   children: React.ReactNode;
     7   /** 降级 UI 标题，默认"此区域发生错误" */
     8   title?: string;
     9   /** 是否显示完整错误信息（建议仅开发环境） */
    10   showDetail?: boolean;
    11   /** 降级 UI 的最小高度样式，用于嵌套在面板内 */
    12   className?: string;
    13 }
    14 
    15 interface ErrorBoundaryState {
    16   hasError: boolean;
    17   error: Error | null;
    18 }
    19 
    20 /**
    21  * 通用错误边界：捕获子组件渲染错误，避免整页白屏。
    22  * 支持嵌套使用（编辑器 / 预览 / 面板各自独立边界）。
    23  */
    24 class ErrorBoundary extends React.Component<ErrorBoundaryProps, ErrorBoundaryState> {
    25   constructor(props: ErrorBoundaryProps) {
    26     super(props);
    27     this.state = { hasError: false, error: null };
    28   }
    29 
    30   static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): ErrorBoundaryState {
    31     return { hasError: true, error };
    32   }
    33 
    34   componentDidCatch(error: Error, info: React.ErrorInfo) {
    35     console.error('[ErrorBoundary] 捕获渲染错误:', error, info.componentStack);
    36   }
    37 
    38   handleReset = () => {
    39     this.setState({ hasError: false, error: null });
    40   };
    41 
    42   render() {
    43     if (!this.state.hasError) {
    44       return this.props.children;
    45     }
    46 
    47     const { title = '此区域发生错误', showDetail = false, className = '' } = this.props;
    48 
    49     return (
    50       <div
    51         className={`flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-3 p-6 text-center min-h-[120px] ${className}`}
    52       >
    53         <AlertTriangle size={24} className="text-destructive shrink-0" />
    54         <div>
    55           <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">{title}</p>
    56           <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">组件渲染出现异常，可尝试刷新或重置</p>
    57           {showDetail && this.state.error && (
    58             <pre className="mt-2 text-left text-[10px] text-muted-foreground bg-muted rounded p-2 max-w-xs overflow-x-auto">
    59               {this.state.error.message}
    60             </pre>
    61           )}
    62         </div>
    63         <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="gap-1.5 h-7" onClick={this.handleReset}>
    64           <RotateCcw size={12} />
    65           重置
    66         </Button>
    67       </div>
    68     );
    69   }
    70 }
    71 
    72 export default ErrorBoundary;
    73

     1 import { useEffect } from 'react';
     2 import { useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
     3 import { Observer } from 'tailwindcss-intersect';
     4 
     5 const IntersectObserver = () => {
     6   const location = useLocation();
     7 
     8   useEffect(() => {
     9     // When the location changes, we need to restart the observer
    10     // to pick up new elements on the page.
    11     // We use a small timeout to ensure the DOM has updated.
    12     const timer = setTimeout(() => {
    13         Observer.restart();
    14     }, 100);
    15 
    16     return () => clearTimeout(timer);
    17   }, [location]);
    18 
    19   return null;
    20 };
